# Scan Report: VA.gov —

- Issue: https://github.com/mgifford/open-scans/issues/167
- Submitted by: mgifford
- Scanned at: 2026-03-16T14:50:32.221Z
- Engines used: All engines (AXE, ALFA, Equal Access, AccessLint, QualWeb)
- Scan duration: 33.8 minutes
- Total URLs submitted: 100
- Accepted public URLs: 100
- Rejected URLs: 0
- 🎨 **Accessibility personalization (CSS media queries):**
  - 🌙 Dark mode: None of the scanned URLs support `prefers-color-scheme: dark`
  - ⚡ Reduced motion: None of the scanned URLs support `prefers-reduced-motion: reduce`
  - 🔍 High contrast: None of the scanned URLs support `prefers-contrast: more`
  - 🖥️ **Forced colors:** 7 of 100 URLs (7%) support `forced-colors: active`
  - 🪟 Reduced transparency: None of the scanned URLs support `prefers-reduced-transparency: reduce`
- ALFA outcomes: 130396 passed, 6537 failed, 748 cantTell, 4337 inapplicable
- axe outcomes: 83518 passed, 6 failed, 3080 cantTell, 4454 inapplicable
- Equal Access outcomes: 218198 passed, 1223 failed (1093 unique, 130 duplicate), 1057 cantTell, 0 inapplicable
- AccessLint outcomes: 8677 passed, 523 failed (522 unique, 1 duplicate), 0 cantTell, 0 inapplicable
- QualWeb outcomes: 47906 passed, 2353 failed, 18170 cantTell, 104 inapplicable
- Duplicate findings caught by later scanners: 7582

## 🔍 Cross-Page Patterns: Common HTML Issues

These HTML patterns cause the same accessibility errors across multiple pages. **Fix the pattern once in your codebase to fix it everywhere!**

### 🎯 Top Patterns to Fix (Highest Impact)

#### Pattern 1: Affects 98 page(s) - 98 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: ALFA
**Rule**: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)
**Issue**: Target has insufficient size

**HTML Pattern**:
```html
<a class="usa-breadcrumb__link" href="/" lang="en-US" hreflang="en-US">...</a>
```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):
```
/a[@class="usa-breadcrumb__link"]
```

**How to Replicate**:
1. Open any affected page in your browser
2. Press F12 to open DevTools
3. Go to Console tab
4. Run: `$x('/a[@class="usa-breadcrumb__link"]')`
5. The element will be highlighted

**Affected Pages**:
- https://va.gov/cheyenne-health-care/stories/caregivers-find-support-community-and-services-at-va/
- https://va.gov/eastern-colorado-health-care/stories/caregivers-find-support-community-and-services-at-va/
- https://va.gov/eastern-oklahoma-health-care/stories/caregivers-find-support-community-and-services-at-va/
- https://va.gov/montana-health-care/stories/caregivers-find-support-community-and-services-at-va/
- https://va.gov/oklahoma-city-health-care/stories/caregivers-find-support-community-and-services-at-va/
- *...and 93 more page(s)*

## Detailed Failure Information (ALFA)

### https://va.gov/cheyenne-health-care/stories/caregivers-find-support-community-and-services-at-va/

#### Rule: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)
**WCAG**: [SC 2.5.8](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/target-size-minimum) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<button class="va-crisis-line va-overlay-trigger vads-u-background-color--secondary-darkest" data-show="#modal-crisisline">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="va-crisis-line va-overlay-trigger vads-u-background-color--secondary-darkest"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<button class="sitewide-search-drop-down-panel-button va-btn-withicon va-dropdown-trigger va-btn-withicon va-dropdown-trigger" aria-controls="search" aria-expanded="false">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="sitewide-search-drop-down-panel-button va-btn-withicon va-dropdown-trigger va-btn-withicon va-dropdown-trigger"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="vads-u-color--white vads-u-text-decoration--none vads-u-padding-x--1 vads-u-font-weight--bold" href="https://www.va.gov/contact-us/">Contact us</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="vads-u-color--white vads-u-text-decoration--none vads-u-padding-x--1 vads-u-font-weight--bold"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<button class="usa-button" type="button" part="button">Sign in</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="usa-button"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="usa-breadcrumb__link" href="/" lang="en-US" hreflang="en-US">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="usa-breadcrumb__link"]`

*... and 1 more failures for this rule*

#### Rule: [SIA-R14: Images have an accessible name or are decorative](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r14)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.1.1](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/non-text-content) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The visible text content of the element is not included within its accessible name
- HTML: `<a aria-label="TTY: 7 1 1." href="tel:+1711">TTY: 711</a>`
- XPath: `/a`

#### Rule: [SIA-R66: Text has enhanced contrast with its background](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r66)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.6](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/contrast-enhanced) (Level AAA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 5.95:1 which is         below the required contrast of 7:1

#### Rule: [SIA-R74](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r74)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p>An official website of the United States governmen...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

**Failure 1:**

**WCAG**: [SC 1.3.1](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/info-and-relationships) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: There is no content between this heading and the next
- HTML: `<h3 class="va-nav-linkslist-title vads-u-font-size--h4" id="-1">...</h3>`
- XPath: `/h3[@id="-1"]`

### https://va.gov/augusta-health-care/programs/first-responder-deflection-support-services/

**WCAG**: [SC 2.5.8](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/target-size-minimum) (Level AA)

- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 5.95:1 which is         below the required contrast of 7:1

#### Rule: [SIA-R71](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r71)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The text of the paragraph is justified
- HTML: `<p>...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

#### Rule: [SIA-R74](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r74)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p>An official website of the United States governmen...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

#### Rule: [SIA-R78: Headings of same level have text content between them](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r78)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.3.1](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/info-and-relationships) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: There is no content between this heading and the next
- HTML: `<h2 id="connect-with-the-local-caregiv">...</h2>`
- XPath: `/h2[@id="connect-with-the-local-caregiv"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: There is no content between this heading and the next
- HTML: `<h3 class="va-nav-linkslist-title vads-u-font-size--h4" id="-1">...</h3>`
- XPath: `/h3[@id="-1"]`

- Message: The visible text content of the element is not included within its accessible name
- HTML: `<a href="tel:+18552603274" aria-label="8 5 5. 2 6 0. 3 2 7 4.">855-260-3274</a>`
- XPath: `/a`

**Failure 1:**

**Failure 1:**

#### Rule: [SIA-R66: Text has enhanced contrast with its background](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r66)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.6](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/contrast-enhanced) (Level AAA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 5.95:1 which is         below the required contrast of 7:1

#### Rule: [SIA-R71](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r71)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The text of the paragraph is justified
- HTML: `<p>...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

#### Rule: [SIA-R74](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r74)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p>An official website of the United States governmen...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

#### Rule: [SIA-R78: Headings of same level have text content between them](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r78)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.3.1](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/info-and-relationships) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: There is no content between this heading and the next
- HTML: `<h3 class="va-nav-linkslist-title vads-u-font-size--h4" id="-1">...</h3>`
- XPath: `/h3[@id="-1"]`

### https://va.gov/columbia-south-carolina-health-care/health-services/caregiver-support/

#### Rule: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)
**WCAG**: [SC 2.5.8](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/target-size-minimum) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<button class="va-crisis-line va-overlay-trigger vads-u-background-color--secondary-darkest" data-show="#modal-crisisline" id="780dae929335de25f16769516c335c3f">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@id="780dae929335de25f16769516c335c3f"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<button class="sitewide-search-drop-down-panel-button va-btn-withicon va-dropdown-trigger va-btn-withicon va-dropdown-trigger" aria-controls="search" aria-expanded="false">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="sitewide-search-drop-down-panel-button va-btn-withicon va-dropdown-trigger va-btn-withicon va-dropdown-trigger"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="vads-u-color--white vads-u-text-decoration--none vads-u-padding-x--1 vads-u-font-weight--bold" href="https://www.va.gov/contact-us/">Contact us</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="vads-u-color--white vads-u-text-decoration--none vads-u-padding-x--1 vads-u-font-weight--bold"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<button class="usa-button" type="button" part="button">Sign in</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="usa-button"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="usa-breadcrumb__link" href="/" lang="en-US" hreflang="en-US">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="usa-breadcrumb__link"]`

- HTML: `<button class="va-crisis-line va-overlay-trigger vads-u-background-color--secondary-darkest" data-show="#modal-crisisline" id="4662fb527edfa4fc2135336a4d2130bd">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@id="4662fb527edfa4fc2135336a4d2130bd"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<button class="sitewide-search-drop-down-panel-button va-btn-withicon va-dropdown-trigger va-btn-withicon va-dropdown-trigger" aria-controls="search" aria-expanded="false">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="sitewide-search-drop-down-panel-button va-btn-withicon va-dropdown-trigger va-btn-withicon va-dropdown-trigger"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="vads-u-color--white vads-u-text-decoration--none vads-u-padding-x--1 vads-u-font-weight--bold" href="https://www.va.gov/contact-us/">Contact us</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="vads-u-color--white vads-u-text-decoration--none vads-u-padding-x--1 vads-u-font-weight--bold"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<button class="usa-button" type="button" part="button">Sign in</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="usa-button"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="usa-breadcrumb__link" href="/" lang="en-US" hreflang="en-US">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="usa-breadcrumb__link"]`

*... and 4 more failures for this rule*

#### Rule: [SIA-R14: Images have an accessible name or are decorative](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r14)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.1.1](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/non-text-content) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The visible text content of the element is not included within its accessible name
- HTML: `<a href="tel:+18552603274" aria-label="8 5 5. 2 6 0. 3 2 7 4.">855-260-3274</a>`
- XPath: `/a`

#### Rule: [SIA-R61](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r61)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The document does not start with a level 1 heading

#### Rule: [SIA-R66: Text has enhanced contrast with its background](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r66)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.6](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/contrast-enhanced) (Level AAA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 5.95:1 which is         below the required contrast of 7:1

#### Rule: [SIA-R71](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r71)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The text of the paragraph is justified
- HTML: `<p>...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

#### Rule: [SIA-R74](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r74)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The font size is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p>An official website of the United States governmen...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

#### Rule: [SIA-R78: Headings of same level have text content between them](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r78)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.3.1](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/info-and-relationships) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: There is no content between this heading and the next
- HTML: `<h3 class="va-nav-linkslist-title vads-u-font-size--h4" id="-1">...</h3>`
- XPath: `/h3[@id="-1"]`

- XPath: `/button[@class="sitewide-search-drop-down-panel-button va-btn-withicon va-dropdown-trigger va-btn-withicon va-dropdown-trigger"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="vads-u-color--white vads-u-text-decoration--none vads-u-padding-x--1 vads-u-font-weight--bold" href="https://www.va.gov/contact-us/">Contact us</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="vads-u-color--white vads-u-text-decoration--none vads-u-padding-x--1 vads-u-font-weight--bold"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<button class="usa-button" type="button" part="button">Sign in</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="usa-button"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="usa-breadcrumb__link" href="/" lang="en-US" hreflang="en-US">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="usa-breadcrumb__link"]`

## Detailed Failure Information (axe)

### https://va.gov/accessibility-at-va-esp/

#### Rule: [aria-dialog-name](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/aria-dialog-name?application=playwright)
**Impact**: serious

**Failure 1:**
- Message: ARIA dialog and alertdialog nodes should have an accessible name
- HTML: `<div aria-modal="true" role="dialog" aria-labelledby="sidebar_header">`
- XPath: `div[aria-modal="true"]`

### https://va.gov/accessibility-at-va/

- Message: ARIA dialog and alertdialog nodes should have an accessible name

### https://va.gov/augusta-health-care/programs/first-responder-deflection-support-services/

#### Rule: [heading-order](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/heading-order?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Heading levels should only increase by one
- HTML: `<h6><strong>Emergency Services at VA Augusta’s Medical Center&nbsp;</strong></h6>`
- XPath: `h6:nth-child(1)`
